new Set();\n  private digitHandlers: Set<(d: string) => void> = new Set();\n  private commandHandlers: Set<(c: string) => void> = new Set();\n  private navigationHandler: ((action: string) => void) | null = null;\n  \n  private constructor() {}\n  \n  static getInstance(): VoiceBrain {\n    if (!VoiceBrain.instance) {\n      VoiceBrain.instance = new VoiceBrain();\n    }\n    return VoiceBrain.instance;\n  }\n  \n  init(): void {\n    if (this.initialized) return;\n    \n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n      this.updateState({ error: 'Speech not supported. Use Chrome.' });\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    this.synth = window.speechSynthesis;\n    this.recognition = new SR();\n    this.recognition.continuous = true;\n    this.recognition.interimResults = true;\n    this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n    \n    this.recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] \u2705 LISTENING');\n      this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING', error: null });\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      const isFinal = result.isFinal;\n      \n      if (isFinal && text) {\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Heard:', text);\n        this.updateState({ transcript: text, interim: '', lastCommand: text });\n        this.processCommand(text.toLowerCase());\n      } else {\n        this.updateState({ interim: text });\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Error:', event.error);\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', error: 'Mic blocked. Click \ud83d\udd12 \u2192 Allow' });\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\n            try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else if (this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.initialized = true;\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \u2705 Initialized');\n  }\n  \n  private updateState(partial: Partial<VoiceBrainState>): void {\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\n  }\n  \n  private processCommand(text: string): void {\n    // Pause commands with empathy\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text.includes('stop') || text.includes('pause') || text.includes('wait')) {\n      this.pause();\n      this.speak(\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume or tap the button to continue.\", 'neutral');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Resume\n    if (text.includes('resume') || text.includes('continue') || text.includes('go ahead')) {\n      this.resume();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Help\n    if (text.includes('help') || text.includes('what can you do')) {\n      this.speak(\"I can help you navigate VistaView. Say things like: sign in, go back, clear, yes to confirm, or speak numbers for phone entry.\", 'happy');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Navigation commands\n    const navCommands: Record<string, string> = {\n      'sign in': 'signin', 'login': 'signin', 'log in': 'signin',\n      'vendor': 'vendor', \"i'm a vendor\": 'vendor', 'im a vendor': 'vendor',\n      'go back': 'back', 'back': 'back', 'previous': 'back',\n      'close': 'close', 'cancel': 'close', 'exit': 'close',\n      'next': 'next', 'continue': 'next', 'submit': 'next',\n      'home': 'home', 'go home': 'home',\n      'about': 'about', 'how it works': 'howitworks',\n      'partners': 'partners', 'lend': 'lend'\n    };\n    \n    for (const [phrase, action] of Object.entries(navCommands)) {\n      if (text.includes(phrase)) {\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Navigation:', action);\n        this.navigationHandler?.(action);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Extract digits\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\n    if (digits) {\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\n    }\n    \n    // Send to command handlers\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\n  }\n  \n  // Public API\n  getState(): VoiceBrainState { return this.state; }\n  \n  subscribe(listener: (s: VoiceBrainState) => void): () => void {\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\n    listener(this.state);\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\n  }\n  \n  onDigits(handler: (d: string) => void): () => void {\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n  \n  onCommand(handler: (c: string) => void): () => void {\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n  \n  setNavigationHandler(handler: (action: string) => void): void {\n    this.navigationHandler = handler;\n  }\n  \n  setContext(context: string): void {\n    this.updateState({ context });\n  }\n  \n  start(): void {\n    this.init();\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n  }\n  \n  stop(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\n  }\n  \n  pause(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    this.updateState({ state: 'PAUSED' });\n  }\n  \n  resume(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    this.speak(\"I'm listening.\", 'neutral');\n  }\n  \n  speak(text: string, emotion: Emotion = 'neutral', onDone?: () => void): void {\n    if (!text) { onDone?.(); return; }\n    \n    this.init();\n    if (!this.synth) { onDone?.(); return; }\n    \n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \ud83d\udd0a Speaking:', text);\n    \n    // Audio Mutex - stop listening while speaking\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\n    }\n    \n    this.synth.cancel();\n    this.updateState({ state: 'SPEAKING', emotion });\n    \n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    \n    // Adjust for emotion\n    switch (emotion) {\n      case 'happy':\n      case 'excited':\n        utterance.rate = 1.1; utterance.pitch = 1.1; break;\n      case 'concerned':\n        utterance.rate = 0.9; utterance.pitch = 0.9; break;\n      case 'thinking':\n        utterance.rate = 0.85; break;\n      default:\n        utterance.rate = 1.0; utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    }\n    \n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n    \n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n    \n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      this.updateState({ state: wasListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\n      onDone?.();\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    utterance.onerror = () => {\n      this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\n      onDone?.();\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    setTimeout(() => this.synth?.speak(utterance), 50);\n  }\n  \n  stopSpeaking(): void {\n    this.synth?.cancel();\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\n  }\n}\n\n// Export singleton\nexport const voiceBrain = VoiceBrain.getInstance();\nexport default voiceBrain;\nBRAINEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 VoiceBrain.ts\"\n\n# Visual pointer element\nlet pointer: HTMLElement | null = null;\n\nfunction createPointer(): HTMLElement {\n  if (pointer) return pointer;\n  \n  pointer = document.createElement('div');\n  pointer.id pointer;\n}\n\nfunction showPointer(x: number, y: number): void {\n  const p = createPointer();\n  p.style.left = `${x}px`;\n  p.style.top = `${y}px`;\n  p.style.display = 'block';\n}\n\nfunction hidePointer(): void {\n  if (pointer) pointer.style.display = 'none';\n}\n\nasync function walkTo(element: HTMLElement): Promise<void> {\n  const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();\n  const x = rect.left + rect.width / 2;\n  const y = rect.top + rect.height / 2;\n  \n  const p = createPointer();\n  p.style.display = 'block';\n  \n  // Animate from current position to target\n  const startX = parseFloat(p.style.left) || window.innerWidth / 2;\n  const startY = parseFloat(p.style.top) || window.innerHeight / 2;\n  \n  p.style.left = `${startX}px`;\n  p.style.top = `${startY}px`;\n  \n HTMLElement): Promise<void> {\n  // Visual feedback\n  element.style.outline = '3px solid #B8860B';\n  element.style.outlineOffset = '2px';\n  \n  await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200));\n  \n  // Click\n  element.click();\n  \n  await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300));\n  \n  // Remove highlight\n  element.style.outline = '';\n  element.style.outlineOffset = '';\n  \n  hidePointer();\n}\n\nfunction findElement(keywords: string[]): HTMLElement | null {\n  // First try data-testid selectors\n  for (const target of CLICK_TARGETS) {\n    if (keywords.some(k => target.keywords.some(tk => k.includes(tk)))) {\n      const el = document.querySelector(target.selector) as HTMLElement;\n      if (el) return el;\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Try finding by text content\n  const allButtons = document.querySelectorAll('button, a, [role=\"button\"]');\n  for (const btn of allButtons) {\n    const text = btn.textContent?.toLowerCase() || '';\n    if (keywords.some(k => text.includes(k))) {\n      return btn as HTMLElement;\n    }\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\nexport async function handleNavigation(action: string): Promise<boolean> {\n  console.log('[WalkAndClick] Try clicking it directly.`, 'concerned');\n    return false;\n  }\n}\n\n// Initialize\nexport function initWalkAndClick(): void {\n  voiceBrain.setNavigationHandler(handleNavigation);\n VOICE BRAIN - The Central Intelligence\\n// \\n// ONE instance controls ALL voice in VistaView\\n// Features:\\n// - Continuous STT with auto-restart\\n// - TTS with emotion\\n// - Audio Mutex (no overlap)\\n// - Context awareness\\n// - Command routing\\n// - \\\"Hey\\\" pauses with empathy\\n// - Walk & Click support\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\ntype VoiceState = 'IDLE' | 'LISTENING' | 'SPEAKING' | 'PAUSED' | 'THINKING';\\ntype Emotion = 'neutral' | 'happy' | 'thinking' | 'concerned' | 'excited';\\n\\ninterface VoiceBrainState {\\n  state: VoiceState;\\n  transcript: string;\\n  interim: string;\\n  error: string | null;\\n  emotion: Emotion;\\n  context: string;\\n  lastCommand: string;\\n}\\n\\n// Word to digit\\nconst W2D: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0', 'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2', 'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8', 'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport function extractDigits(text: string): string {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const w of words) {\\n    if (W2D[w]) digits += W2D[w];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(w)) digits += w;\\n  }\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n}\\n\\nexport function formatPhone(d: string): string {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0,3)}-${c.slice(3,6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n}\\n\\nclass VoiceBrain {\\n  private static instance: VoiceBrain;\\n  \\n  private recognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\\n  private synth: SpeechSynthesis | null = null;\\n  private initialized = false;\\n  private shouldRestart = true;\\n  \\n  private state: VoiceBrainState = {\\n    state: 'IDLE',\\n    transcript: '',\\n    interim: '',\\n    error: null,\\n    emotion: 'neutral',\\n    context: 'home',\\n    lastCommand: ''\\n  };\\n  \\n  private listeners: Set<(s: VoiceBrainState) => void> = new Set();\\n  private digitHandlers: Set<(d: string) => void> = new Set();\\n  private commandHandlers: Set<(c: string) => void> = new Set();\\n  private navigationHandler: ((action: string) => void) | null = null;\\n  \\n  private constructor() {}\\n  \\n  static getInstance(): VoiceBrain {\\n    if (!VoiceBrain.instance) {\\n      VoiceBrain.instance = new VoiceBrain();\\n    }\\n    return VoiceBrain.instance;\\n  }\\n  \\n  init(): void {\\n    if (this.initialized) return;\\n    \\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) {\\n      this.updateState({ error: 'Speech not supported. Use Chrome.' });\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    this.synth = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    this.recognition = new SR();\\n    this.recognition.continuous = true;\\n    this.recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\u2705 LISTENING');\\n      this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING', error: null });\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      const isFinal = result.isFinal;\\n      \\n      if (isFinal && text) {\\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Heard:', text);\\n        this.updateState({ transcript: text, interim: '', lastCommand: text });\\n        this.processCommand(text.toLowerCase());\\n      } else {\\n        this.updateState({ interim: text });\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', error: 'Mic blocked. Click \\ud83d\\udd12 \\u2192 Allow' });\\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\\n            try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else if (this.state.state !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.state !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.initialized = true;\\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\u2705 Initialized');\\n  }\\n  \\n  private updateState(partial: Partial<VoiceBrainState>): void {\\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\\n  }\\n  \\n  private processCommand(text: string): void {\\n    // Pause commands with empathy\\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text.includes('stop') || text.includes('pause') || text.includes('wait')) {\\n      this.pause();\\n      this.speak(\\\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume or tap the button to continue.\\\", 'neutral');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Resume\\n    if (text.includes('resume') || text.includes('continue') || text.includes('go ahead')) {\\n      this.resume();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Help\\n    if (text.includes('help') || text.includes('what can you do')) {\\n      this.speak(\\\"I can help you navigate VistaView. Say things like: sign in, go back, clear, yes to confirm, or speak numbers for phone entry.\\\", 'happy');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Navigation commands\\n    const navCommands: Record<string, string> = {\\n      'sign in': 'signin', 'login': 'signin', 'log in': 'signin',\\n      'vendor': 'vendor', \\\"i'm a vendor\\\": 'vendor', 'im a vendor': 'vendor',\\n      'go back': 'back', 'back': 'back', 'previous': 'back',\\n      'close': 'close', 'cancel': 'close', 'exit': 'close',\\n      'next': 'next', 'continue': 'next', 'submit': 'next',\\n      'home': 'home', 'go home': 'home',\\n      'about': 'about', 'how it works': 'howitworks',\\n      'partners': 'partners', 'lend': 'lend'\\n    };\\n    \\n    for (const [phrase, action] of Object.entries(navCommands)) {\\n      if (text.includes(phrase)) {\\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Navigation:', action);\\n        this.navigationHandler?.(action);\\n        return;\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract digits\\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n    if (digits) {\\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Send to command handlers\\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\\n  }\\n  \\n  // Public API\\n  getState(): VoiceBrainState { return this.state; }\\n  \\n  subscribe(listener: (s: VoiceBrainState) => void): () => void {\\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\\n    listener(this.state);\\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\\n  }\\n  \\n  onDigits(handler: (d: string) => void): () => void {\\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\\n  }\\n  \\n  onCommand(handler: (c: string) => void): () => void {\\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\\n  }\\n  \\n  setNavigationHandler(handler: (action: string) => void): void {\\n    this.navigationHandler = handler;\\n  }\\n  \\n  setContext(context: string): void {\\n    this.updateState({ context });\\n  }\\n  \\n  start(): void {\\n    this.init();\\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  stop(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE' });\\n  }\\n  \\n  pause(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'PAUSED' });\\n  }\\n  \\n  resume(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'LISTENING' });\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.speak(\\\"I'm listening.\\\", 'neutral');\\n  }\\n  \\n  speak(text: string, emotion: Emotion = 'neutral', onDone?: () => void): void {\\n    if (!text) { onDone?.(); return; }\\n    \\n    this.init();\\n    if (!this.synth) { onDone?.(); return; }\\n    \\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking:', text);\\n    \\n    // Audio Mutex - stop listening while speaking\\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    this.synth.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'SPEAKING', emotion });\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    \\n    // Adjust for emotion\\n    switch (emotion) {\\n      case 'happy':\\n      case 'excited':\\n        utterance.rate = 1.1; utterance.pitch = 1.1; break;\\n      case 'concerned':\\n        utterance.rate = 0.9; utterance.pitch = 0.9; break;\\n      case 'thinking':\\n        utterance.rate = 0.85; break;\\n      default:\\n        utterance.rate = 1.0; utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    }\\n    \\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n    \\n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n    \\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      this.updateState({ state: wasListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\\n      onDone?.();\\n      if (wasListening) {\\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    utterance.onerror = () => {\\n      this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\\n      onDone?.();\\n      if (wasListening) {\\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    setTimeout(() => this.synth?.speak(utterance), 50);\\n  }\\n  \\n  stopSpeaking(): void {\\n    this.synth?.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'IDLE', emotion: 'neutral' });\\n  }\\n}\\n\\n// Export singleton\\nexport const voiceBrain = VoiceBrain.getInstance();\\nexport default voiceBrain;\\nBRAINEOF\\n\\necho \\\" \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n// AGENTIC BAR - The Unified Voice Interface\\n// Use this in EVERY page, modal, popup\\n// \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nimport React, { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react';\\nimport { voiceBrain, extractDigits, formatPhone } from './VoiceBrain';\\n\\nexport { extractDigits, formatPhone };\\n\\n// Hook for components\\nexport function useVoice() {\\n  const [state, setState] = useState(voiceBrain.getState());\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    voiceBrain.init();\\n    return voiceBrain.subscribe(setState);\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  return {\\n    ...state,\\n    isListening: state.state === 'LISTENING',\\n    isSpeaking: state.state === 'SPEAKING',\\n    isPaused: state.state === 'PAUSED',\\n    start: () => voiceBrain.start(),\\n    stop: () => voiceBrain.stop(),\\n    pause: () => voiceBrain.pause(),\\n    resume: () => voiceBrain.resume(),\\n    speak: (text: string, voiceBrain.onDigits(h),\\n    onCommand: (h: (c: string) => void) => voiceBrain.onCommand(h),\\n    setContext: (c: string) => voiceBrain.setContext(c)\\n  };\\n}\\n\\n// Global functions for easy access\\nexport const speak = (text: string, emotion?: any, onDone?: () => void) => voiceBrain.speak(text, emotion, onDone);\\nexport const startListening = () => voiceBrain.start();\\nexport const stopListening = () => voiceBrain.stop();\\nexport const pauseListening = () => voiceBrain.pause();\\nexport const resumeListening = () => voiceBrain.resume();\\nexport const onDigits = (h: (d: string) => void) => voiceBrain.onDigits(h);\\nexport const onCommand = (h: (c: string) => void) => voiceBrain.onCommand(h);\\nexport const setContext = (c: string) => voiceBrain.setContext(c);\\nexport const setNavigationHandler = (h: (a: string) => void) => voiceBrain.setNavigationHandler(h);\\n\\ninterface AgenticBarProps {\\n  context?: string;\\n  hints?: string[];\\n  welcomeMessage?: string;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n  compact?: boolean;\\n  onDigits?: (d: string) => void;\\n  onCommand?: (c: string) => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst AgenticBar: React.FC<AgenticBarProps> = ({\\n  context,\\n  hints,\\n  welcomeMessage,\\n  autoStart = true,\\n  compact = false,\\n  onDigits: onDigitsProp,\\n  onCommand: onCommandProp\\n}) => {\\n  const voice = useVoice();\\n  const welcomeSpoken = useRef(false);\\n  \\n  // Register handlers\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (onDigitsProp) return voiceBrain.onDigits(onDigitsProp);\\n  }, [onDigitsProp]);\\n  \\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (onCommandProp) return voiceBrain.onCommand(onCommandProp);\\n  }, [onCommandProp]);\\n  \\n  // Set context\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (context) voiceBrain.setContext(context);\\n  }, [context]);\\n  \\n  // Welcome + auto-start\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!welcomeSpoken.current) {\\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\\n      if (welcomeMessage) {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          voiceBrain.speak(welcomeMessage, 'happy', () => {\\n            if (autoStart) voiceBrain.start();\\n          });\\n        }, 500);\\n      } else if (autoStart) {\\n        setTimeout(() => voiceBrain.start(), 500);\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }, [welcomeMessage, autoStart]);\\n  \\n  const statusColor = voice.isSpeaking ? '#FFD700' : voice.isListening ? '#4CAF50' : voice.isPaused ? '#FF9800' : '#f44336';\\n  const statusText = voice.isSpeaking ? '\\ud83d\\udd0a Speaking...' : voice.isListening ? '\\ud83c\\udfa4 Listening...' : voice.isPaused ? '\\u23f8\\ufe0f Paused' : '\\u25a0 Stopped';\\n  \\n  if (compact) {\\n    return (\\n      <div style={{\\n        display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px',\\n        padding: '8px 14px', background: `rgba(${voice.isListening ? '76,175,80' : '244,67,54'},0.15)`,\\n        border: `2px solid ${statusColor}`, borderRadius: '20px', cursor: 'pointer'\\n      }} onClick={() => voice.isPaused || !voice.isListening ? voiceBrain.start() : voiceBrain.pause()}>\\n        <span style={{ width: '10px', height: '10px', borderRadius: '50%', background: statusColor,\\n          animation: voice.isListening ? 'ab-pulse 1.5s infinite' : 'none' }} />\\n        <span style={{ color: statusColor, fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '0.9em' }}>{statusText}</span>\\n        <style>{`@keyframes ab-pulse { 0%,100% { opacity:1; } 50% { opacity:0.4; } }`}</style>\\n      </div>\\n    );\\n  }\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <div style={{\\n      margin: '16px 0 0', padding: '14px 16px',\\n      background: voice.isListening ? 'rgba(76,175,80,0.12)' : voice.isSpeaking ? 'rgba(255,215,0,0.1)' : 'rgba(244,67,54,0.08)',\\n      border: `2px solid ${statusColor}`, borderRadius: '14px'\\n    }}>\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>\\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '10px' }}>\\n          <span style={{ width: '14px', height: '14px', borderRadius: '50%', background: statusColor,\\n            boxShadow: voice.isListening ? `0 0 10px ${statusColor}` : 'none',\\n            animation: voice.isListening ? 'ab-pulse 1.5s infinite' : 'none' }} />\\n          <span style={{ color: statusColor, fontWeight: 600 }}>{statusText}</span>\\n          {context && <span style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\\u2022 {context}</span>}\\n        </div>\\n        \\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}>\\n          {voice.isPaused ? '#888' : '#4CAF50', fontSize: '0.7em', marginBottom: '4px' }}>\\n            {voice.interim ?
